---
title     : "TypedBarendregt: Raw terms with types (broken)"
layout    : page
permalink : /TypedBarendregt
---

This version uses raw terms. Substitution presumes that no
generation of fresh names is required.

The substitution algorithm is based on one by McBride.
It is given a map from names to terms. Say the mapping of a
name is trivial if it takes a name to a term consisting of
just the variable with that name. No fresh names are required
if the mapping on each variable is either trivial or to a
closed term. However, the proof of correctness currently
contains a hole, and may be difficult to repair.

## Values do not reduce

Values do not reduce.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Val-⟶"></a><a id="12944" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12950" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12952" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12954" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12955" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12957" class="Bound">N</a><a id="12958" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12960" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9189" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="12968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12955" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12970" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12972" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="12974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12955" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9456" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="12979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12957" class="Bound">N</a><a id="12980" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9339" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="12992" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="12995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9217" class="InductiveConstructor">Zero</a> <a id="13006" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="13009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13015" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9262" class="InductiveConstructor">Suc</a> <a id="13020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13020" class="Bound">VM</a><a id="13022" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13024" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9771" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="13031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13031" class="Bound">M⟶N</a><a id="13034" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="13037" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="13040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13020" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="13049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13031" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As a corollary, terms that reduce are not values.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⟶-Val"></a><a id="13128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13128" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="13134" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13136" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13138" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13139" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13141" class="Bound">N</a><a id="13142" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13144" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13146" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13139" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9456" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="13151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13141" class="Bound">N</a><a id="13152" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13154" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13156" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="13158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9189" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="13164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13139" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="13166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13128" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="13172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13172" class="Bound">M⟶N</a> <a id="13176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13176" class="Bound">VM</a>  <a id="13180" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="13183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13189" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13176" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="13192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13172" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Reduction is deterministic

  <a id="13272" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13274" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13261" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9456" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="13279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13263" class="Bound">M′</a><a id="13281" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="14774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13252" class="Function">det</a> <a id="14778" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#10532" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="14783" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="14787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14789" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14790" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#10532" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="14794" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="14798" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14800" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14802" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Almost half the lines in the above proof are redundant, for example

    det (ξ-·₁ L⟶L′) (ξ-·₂ VL _) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L′)
    det (ξ-·₂ VL _) (ξ-·₁ L⟶L″) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L″)
 
are essentially identical. What we might like to do is delete the
redundant lines and add

    det M⟶M′ M⟶M″ = sym (det M⟶M″ M⟶M′)

to the bottom of the proof. But this does not work. The termination
checker complains, because the arguments have merely switched order
and neither is smaller.

## Canonical forms

## Progress

## Preservation

### Domain of an environment

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17886" class="Comment">{-
dom : Ctx → List Id
dom ε            =  []
dom (Γ , x `: A)  =  x ∷ dom Γ

dom-lemma : ∀ {Γ y B} → Γ ∋ y `: B → y ∈ dom Γ
dom-lemma Z           =  here
dom-lemma (S x≢y ⊢y)  =  there (dom-lemma ⊢y)

free-lemma : ∀ {Γ M A} → Γ ⊢ M `: A → free M ⊆ dom Γ
free-lemma (Ax ⊢x) w∈ with w∈
...                      | here         =  dom-lemma ⊢x
...                      | there ()   
free-lemma {Γ} (⊢λ {N = N} ⊢N)          =  ∷-to-\\ (free-lemma ⊢N)
free-lemma (⊢L · ⊢M) w∈ with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...                        | inj₁ ∈L    = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...                        | inj₂ ∈M    = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
free-lemma ⊢zero ()
free-lemma (⊢suc ⊢M) w∈                 = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢pred ⊢M) w∈                = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢if0 ⊢L ⊢M ⊢N) w∈
        with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...         | inj₁ ∈L                   = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...         | inj₂ ∈MN with ++-to-⊎ ∈MN
...                       | inj₁ ∈M     = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
...                       | inj₂ ∈N     = free-lemma ⊢N ∈N
free-lemma (⊢Y ⊢M) w∈                   = free-lemma ⊢M w∈       
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Substitution preserves types

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21716" class="Comment">{-
⊢subst : ∀ {Γ Δ ρ}
  → (∀ {x A} → Δ ∋ x `: A  →  Γ ∋ x `: A)
  → (∀ {x A} → Γ ∋ x `: A  →  Δ ⊢ ρ x `: A)
    --------------------------------------------------------------
  → (∀ {M A} → (⊢M : Γ ⊢ M `: A) →  ok ⊢M  →  Δ ⊢ subst ρ M `: A)
-}</a>
<a id="⊢subst"></a><a id="21960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21960" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="21967" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21969" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21971" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21972" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="21974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21974" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="21976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21976" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="21977" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="23059" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="23062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢if0</a> <a id="23067" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21960" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23075" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23036" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23078" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23045" class="Bound">⊢L</a><a id="23080" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23082" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21960" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23090" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23036" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23093" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23048" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23095" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23097" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21960" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23036" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23051" class="Bound">⊢N</a><a id="23110" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="23112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21960" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23119" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#3025" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="23126" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23126" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23128" class="Symbol">)</a>                <a id="23145" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="23148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#3025" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="23151" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23152" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21960" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23119" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23126" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23164" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let's look at examples.  Assume `M` is closed.  Example 1.

    subst (tm-∅ , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x")  ≡  `λ "y" `→ M

Example 2.

      subst (tm-∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ subst (tm-∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M , "y" ↦ ` "y") (` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ (M · ` "y")

The hypotheses of the theorem appear to be violated. Drat!

  <a id="23612" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23597" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="23616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#1756" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23599" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#1756" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`:</a> <a id="23623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23601" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#2309" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="23627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23603" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="23629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#2309" class="Datatype Operator">`:</a> <a id="23632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23605" class="Bound">B</a>
